//#startcode

campaignTrail_temp.cyoa = true;

// pk -> index lookup for questions
let _questionIdxByPk = null;

function _rebuildQuestionIdxMap() {
  _questionIdxByPk = new Map();
  const arr = campaignTrail_temp.questions_json;
  for (let i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) {
    _questionIdxByPk.set(Number(arr[i].pk), i);
  }
}

// returns the true array index (>= 0) or -1 if not found
function getQuestionIndexFromPk(pk) {
  const n = Number(pk);
  if (!_questionIdxByPk) _rebuildQuestionIdxMap();

  let idx = _questionIdxByPk.get(n);
  // if map is stale, rebuild once
  if (idx == null || campaignTrail_temp.questions_json[idx]?.pk !== n) {
    _rebuildQuestionIdxMap();
    idx = _questionIdxByPk.get(n);
  }
  return idx ?? -1;
}

// index to assign into question_number before nextQuestion()
function getJumpIndexFromPk(pk) {
  const idx = getQuestionIndexFromPk(pk);
  return idx >= 0 ? idx - 1 : -1;
}

// for backwards compatibility
function getQuestionNumberFromPk(pk) {
  return getJumpIndexFromPk(pk);
}

function questionSwapper(pk1, pk2) {
    const questionData = campaignTrail_temp.questions_json;
    
    // find indices of the questions
    const index1 = getQuestionIndexFromPk(pk1);
    const index2 = getQuestionIndexFromPk(pk2);
    
    // validate both questions exist
    if (index1 === -1 || index2 === -1) {
        console.warn(`questionSwapper: Could not find question(s) with pk ${pk1} and/or ${pk2}`);
        return false;
    }
    
    // swap the entire question objects
    [questionData[index1], questionData[index2]] = [questionData[index2], questionData[index1]];
    
    // rebuild the index map since positions changed
    _rebuildQuestionIdxMap();
    
    return true;
}

function answerSwapper(pk1, pk2, takeEffects = true) {
    const answerData = campaignTrail_temp.answers_json;

   // find the indices of the objects with the specified PKs
    const index1 = answerData.findIndex(item => Number(item.pk) === Number(pk1));
    const index2 = answerData.findIndex(item => Number(item.pk) === Number(pk2));

    // check if objects with those PKs exist
    if (index1 === -1 || index2 === -1) return;

    // swap the question assignment
    const tempQuestion = answerData[index1].fields.question;
    answerData[index1].fields.question = answerData[index2].fields.question;
    answerData[index2].fields.question = tempQuestion;

    // if takeEffects is true, answers swap effects also
    if (takeEffects) {
        const otherJsons = [
            campaignTrail_temp.answer_score_global_json,
            campaignTrail_temp.answer_score_issue_json,
            campaignTrail_temp.answer_score_state_json,
            campaignTrail_temp.answer_feedback_json
        ];

        otherJsons.forEach(jsonData => {
            if (!jsonData) return;
            jsonData.forEach(item => {
                const itemAns = Number(item.fields.answer);
                if (itemAns === Number(pk1)) {
                    item.fields.answer = pk2;
                } else if (itemAns === Number(pk2)) {
                    item.fields.answer = pk1;
                }
            });
        });
    }
}

function updateTypewriterVisibility() {
    const mapVisible = !!document.getElementById('resume_questions_button');
    const visitVisible = !!document.querySelector('.visit_text');
    let tw = document.getElementById('typewriter-overlay');
    if (mapVisible || visitVisible) {
        if (tw) tw.style.display = 'none';
        const sign = document.querySelector('#campaign_sign');
        if (sign && sign.parentElement && sign.parentElement.classList.contains('content_single')) {
            sign.style.display = 'none';
        }

        const allSigns = document.querySelectorAll('#campaign_sign');
        allSigns.forEach(s => {
            if (!s.parentElement || !s.parentElement.classList.contains('content_single')) {
                s.style.display = 'none';
            }
        });
        return;
    }
    const gEl = document.querySelector('#game_window g');
    if (!gEl) return;
    if (!tw) {
        tw = document.createElement('div');
        tw.id = 'typewriter-overlay';
        tw.style.cssText = `
            position: absolute;
            bottom: 0;
            left: 50%;
            transform: translateX(-50%);
            width: 989px;
            height: 175px;
            background-image: url('https://file.garden/aXPgNT-ZRCxxpy0g/typewriterv1.png');
            background-size: cover;
            background-position: center;
            background-repeat: no-repeat;
            pointer-events: none;
            z-index: 5;
        `;
        gEl.appendChild(tw);
    }
    tw.style.display = 'block';
    const sign = document.querySelector('#campaign_sign');
    if (sign && sign.parentElement && sign.parentElement.classList.contains('content_single')) {
        sign.style.display = 'block';
    }
}

setInterval(updateTypewriterVisibility, 200);

let imgUrl = "https://file.garden/aXPgNT-ZRCxxpy0g/creepv2.jpg";

const _signStyling = document.createElement("style");
document.head.appendChild(_signStyling);

function updateStyling(url) {
    const img = new Image();
    img.onload = function() {
        const sign = document.querySelector('#campaign_sign');
        const currentLeft = sign ? sign.style.left : '';
        const currentTop = sign ? sign.style.top : '';
        const currentWidth = sign ? sign.style.width : '380px';
        const currentHeight = sign ? sign.style.height : '';
        _signStyling.textContent = `
            #campaign_sign {
                background-image: url("${url}");
                background-size: 100% 100% !important;
                background-position: center !important;
                width: ${currentWidth || img.naturalWidth + 'px'};
                height: ${currentHeight || img.naturalHeight + 'px'};
                font-size: 0;
            }
        `;
        if (sign) {
        }
    };
    img.src = url;
}

updateStyling(imgUrl);

function changeImage(newImgUrl) {
    imgUrl = newImgUrl;

    updateStyling(newImgUrl);
}

let activeSign = null;
let isDraggingSign = false;
let signDragStartX = 0;
let signDragStartY = 0;
let signStartLeft = 0;
let signStartTop = 0;

document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
    if (!isDraggingSign || !activeSign) return;
    const dx = e.clientX - signDragStartX;
    const dy = e.clientY - signDragStartY;
    activeSign.style.left = (signStartLeft + dx) + 'px';
    activeSign.style.top = (signStartTop + dy) + 'px';
});

document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => {
    isDraggingSign = false;
    if (activeSign) {
        activeSign.style.cursor = 'grab';
        savedSignLeft = activeSign.style.left;
        savedSignTop = activeSign.style.top;
    }
});

let savedSignLeft = '';
let savedSignTop = '';

function updateCampaignSign() {
    const sign = document.querySelector('#campaign_sign');
    if (sign && sign !== activeSign) {
        if (activeSign && activeSign.parentElement && activeSign.parentElement.classList.contains('content_single')) {
            activeSign.remove();
        }
        activeSign = sign;
        const contentSingle = document.querySelector('.content_single');
        if (contentSingle && sign.parentElement !== contentSingle) {
            const signRect = sign.getBoundingClientRect();
            const parentRect = contentSingle.getBoundingClientRect();
            contentSingle.appendChild(sign);
            if (!savedSignLeft) {
                sign.style.left = (signRect.left - parentRect.left - 105) + 'px';
                sign.style.top = (signRect.top - parentRect.top + 130) + 'px';
            } else {
                sign.style.left = savedSignLeft;
                sign.style.top = savedSignTop;
            }
            sign.style.position = 'absolute';
        }
        sign.style.cursor = 'grab';
        sign.style.transform = 'rotate(-1.0deg)';
        sign.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
            isDraggingSign = true;
            signDragStartX = e.clientX;
            signDragStartY = e.clientY;
            signStartLeft = parseFloat(sign.style.left) || sign.offsetLeft;
            signStartTop = parseFloat(sign.style.top) || sign.offsetTop;
            sign.style.cursor = 'grabbing';
            e.preventDefault();
        });
        sign.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            e.stopPropagation();
        });
        updateTypewriterVisibility();
    }
}

function addInnerCircleButton() {
    if (document.getElementById('inner_circle_button')) return;
    const ref = document.getElementById('view_electoral_map');
    if (!ref) return;
    const btn = document.createElement('button');
    btn.id = 'inner_circle_button';
    btn.textContent = 'Enemies/Friends';
    btn.style.marginLeft = '10px';
    btn.addEventListener('click', openInnerCircle);
    ref.insertAdjacentElement('afterend', btn);
}

function openInnerCircle() {
    const questions = document.querySelector('.inner_window_question');
    if (questions) questions.style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('inner_circle_button')?.remove();

    const panel = document.createElement('div');
    panel.id = 'inner_circle_panel';

    const title = document.createElement('h2');
    title.textContent = "All the President's Men";
    panel.appendChild(title);

    const chartWrapper = document.createElement('div');
    if (typeof window._renderOrgChart === 'function') window._renderOrgChart(chartWrapper);
    panel.appendChild(chartWrapper);

    const btnRow = document.createElement('div');
    btnRow.className = 'ic-panel-buttons';

    const enemiesBtn = document.createElement('button');
    enemiesBtn.textContent = 'Enemies List';
    enemiesBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        panel.remove();
        openEnemiesPanel(questions);
    });
    btnRow.appendChild(enemiesBtn);

    const backBtn = document.createElement('button');
    backBtn.textContent = 'Back';
    backBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        panel.remove();
        if (questions) questions.style.display = '';
        addInnerCircleButton();
    });
    btnRow.appendChild(backBtn);

    panel.appendChild(btnRow);
    document.getElementById('game_window').appendChild(panel);
    requestAnimationFrame(() => requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        if (typeof window._drawOrgLinks === 'function') window._drawOrgLinks();
    }));
}

function openEnemiesPanel(questions) {
    document.getElementById('enemies_panel')?.remove();

    const panel = document.createElement('div');
    panel.id = 'enemies_panel';

    const title = document.createElement('h2');
    title.textContent = "Enemies List";
    panel.appendChild(title);

    const list = document.createElement('div');
    list.className = 'enemies-list';

    const placeholder = document.createElement('p');
    placeholder.style.fontFamily = "'TypewriterDry', sans-serif";
    placeholder.style.fontSize = '16px';
    placeholder.style.color = '#555';
    placeholder.textContent = '— No enemies tracked yet —';
    list.appendChild(placeholder);

    panel.appendChild(list);

    const btnRow = document.createElement('div');
    btnRow.className = 'ic-panel-buttons';

    const backBtn = document.createElement('button');
    backBtn.textContent = 'Back';
    backBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        panel.remove();
        openInnerCircle();
    });
    btnRow.appendChild(backBtn);
    panel.appendChild(btnRow);

    document.getElementById('game_window').appendChild(panel);
}

        { from: 'Strachan', to: 'Mitchell', color: '#664422', dashed: true },
        { from: 'Hunt',     to: 'Magruder', color: '#664422', dashed: true },
        { from: 'Liddy',    to: 'Magruder', color: '#664422', dashed: true },
        { from: 'Klambach', to: 'Larue',    color: '#665522', dashed: true },

    function _buildOrgNode(id, isCREEP) {
        const p = _orgPeople[id] || { name: id, title: '', bio: '', initials: id.slice(0, 2), images: {} };
        const photo = p.images.active
            ? `<img src="${p.images.active}" alt="${p.name}">`
            : `<span class="nw-initials">${p.initials}</span>`;
        return `<div class="nw-node${isCREEP ? ' nw-creep' : ''}" data-person="${id}" data-state="active">
            <div class="nw-photo-wrap">${photo}</div>
            <div class="nw-name">${p.name}</div>
            <div class="nw-title">${p.title}</div>
            <div class="nw-bio">${p.bio}</div>
        </div>`;
    }

    function _buildOrgTree(node, isCREEP) {
        const kids = (node.children || []).map(c => `<li>${_buildOrgTree(c, isCREEP)}</li>`).join('');
        return _buildOrgNode(node.id, isCREEP) + (kids ? `<ul>${kids}</ul>` : '');
    }

    // Called by openInnerCircle — renders the chart into the supplied wrapper element
    window._renderOrgChart = function(wrapper) {
        wrapper.id = 'nw-chart-wrapper';
        wrapper.innerHTML = `
            <div id="nw-chart-inner">
            <svg id="nw-svg-overlay"></svg>
            <div id="nw-nixon-row">${_buildOrgNode('Nixon', false)}</div>
            <div id="nw-columns-row">
                <div class="nw-col">
                    <div class="nw-col-label">&nbsp;</div>
                    <ul class="nw-tree"><li>${_buildOrgTree({ id: 'Dean' }, false)}</li></ul>
                </div>
                <div class="nw-col">
                    <div class="nw-col-label">White House Staff</div>
                    <ul class="nw-tree"><li>${_buildOrgTree(_whTree1, false)}</li></ul>
                </div>
                <div class="nw-col">
                    <div class="nw-col-label">&nbsp;</div>
                    <ul class="nw-tree"><li>${_buildOrgTree(_whTree2, false)}</li></ul>
                </div>
                <div class="nw-divider"></div>
                <div class="nw-col">
                    <div class="nw-col-label">C.R.E.E.P.</div>
                    <ul class="nw-tree"><li>${_buildOrgTree(_creepTree, true)}</li></ul>
                </div>
            </div>
            </div>
        `;
    };

    window._drawOrgLinks = function() {
        const svg   = document.getElementById('nw-svg-overlay');
        const inner = document.getElementById('nw-chart-inner');
        if (!svg || !inner) return;
        svg.innerHTML = '';
        const cr = inner.getBoundingClientRect();

        const nixonNode = document.querySelector('#nw-nixon-row .nw-node');
        document.querySelectorAll('#nw-columns-row .nw-col .nw-tree > li > .nw-node').forEach(root => {
            _drawOrgArc(svg, cr, nixonNode, root, '#666', false);
        });

        _crossLinks.forEach(({ from, to, color, dashed }) => {
            const a = document.querySelector(`.nw-node[data-person="${from}"]`);
            const b = document.querySelector(`.nw-node[data-person="${to}"]`);
            if (a && b) _drawOrgArc(svg, cr, a, b, color, dashed);
        });
    };

    function _drawOrgArc(svg, cr, elA, elB, color, dashed) {
        const a = elA.getBoundingClientRect();
        const b = elB.getBoundingClientRect();
        const acx = a.left + a.width  / 2 - cr.left;
        const bcx = b.left + b.width  / 2 - cr.left;
        // If source box is clearly above target box, connect bottom-center → top-center.
        // Otherwise (lateral / cross-link) connect the near side-edges at mid-height
        // so the arc visually leaves the card border, not the photo area.
        const isDownward = (a.bottom + 4) < b.top;
        let d;
        if (isDownward) {
            const x1 = acx,           y1 = a.bottom - cr.top;
            const x2 = bcx,           y2 = b.top    - cr.top;
            const cy = (y1 + y2) / 2;
            d = `M ${x1} ${y1} C ${x1} ${cy}, ${x2} ${cy}, ${x2} ${y2}`;
        } else {
            const aIsLeft = acx < bcx;
            const x1 = (aIsLeft ? a.right : a.left) - cr.left;
            const y1 = a.top + a.height / 2 - cr.top;
            const x2 = (aIsLeft ? b.left  : b.right) - cr.left;
            const y2 = b.top + b.height / 2 - cr.top;
            const cmx = (x1 + x2) / 2;
            d = `M ${x1} ${y1} C ${cmx} ${y1}, ${cmx} ${y2}, ${x2} ${y2}`;
        }
        const path = document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg', 'path');
        path.setAttribute('d', d);
        path.setAttribute('stroke', color);
        path.setAttribute('stroke-width', '1.5');
        path.setAttribute('fill', 'none');
        if (dashed) path.setAttribute('stroke-dasharray', '4 3');
        svg.appendChild(path);
    }

    window._setOrgState = function(personId, state) {
        const node = document.querySelector(`.nw-node[data-person="${personId}"]`);
        if (!node) return;
        node.dataset.state = state;
        const p = _orgPeople[personId];
        if (!p) return;
        const img = node.querySelector('img');
        if (img && p.images[state]) img.src = p.images[state];
    };
})();

const _visitAdvisorImages = [
    'https://file.garden/aXPgNT-ZRCxxpy0g/Map%20Pics/planefeedback1.jpg',

];

let _lastQuestionPK = null;
const _gameObserver = new MutationObserver((() => {
    let _pending = false;
    return () => {
        if (_pending) return;
        _pending = true;
        requestAnimationFrame(() => {
            _pending = false;
            updateTypewriterVisibility();
            updateCampaignSign();
            addInnerCircleButton();

            if (typeof e !== 'undefined' && e.question_number != null) {
                const currentPK = campaignTrail_temp.questions_json?.[e.question_number]?.pk ?? null;
                if (currentPK !== _lastQuestionPK) {
                    _lastQuestionPK = currentPK;
                    const qd = (currentPK != null && questionData[currentPK]) || {};
                    if (qd.signImg) changeImage(qd.signImg);
                    if (qd.transition && !_shownTransitions.has(currentPK) && document.getElementById('question_form')) {
                        showSectionTransition(qd.transition, currentPK);
                    }
                    document.querySelectorAll('.game_answer_row').forEach((row, i) => {
                        row.style.setProperty('--answer-i-delay', `${i * 60}ms`);
                    });
                }

                if (_lastQuestionPK != null) {
                    const h3 = document.querySelector('#progress_bar h3');
                    if (h3 && h3.dataset.dateAttached !== String(_lastQuestionPK)) {
                        const qd = questionData[_lastQuestionPK] || {};
                        attachDateToProgressBar(qd.date || '', e.question_number, _lastQuestionPK);
                    }
                }
            }

            const visitImg = document.querySelector('#visit_content img');
            if (visitImg && !visitImg.dataset.visitImgSet && document.querySelector('#confirm_visit_button')) {
                visitImg.dataset.visitImgSet = '1';
                visitImg.src = _visitAdvisorImages[Math.floor(Math.random() * _visitAdvisorImages.length)];
            }

            const noFeedbackBtn = document.getElementById('no_feedback_button');
            if (noFeedbackBtn && !noFeedbackBtn.dataset.historicalHooked) {
                injectHistoricalButton(noFeedbackBtn, _lastQuestionPK);
            }
        });
    };
})());
_gameObserver.observe(document.getElementById('game_window'), { childList: true, subtree: true });

function generatePenStroke() {
    const height = 6;
    const d = 'M 0 0 Q 35 5 50 3 Q 65 1 100 4';
    return `<svg style="position:absolute;bottom:-1px;left:0;width:100%;height:${height}px;overflow:visible;pointer-events:none" preserveAspectRatio="none" viewBox="0 0 100 ${height}"><path d="${d}" fill="none" stroke="rgb(96, 115, 129)" stroke-width="2.1" vector-effect="non-scaling-stroke"/></svg>`;
}

function getTooltips(str) {
    let matches = [];
    tooltipList.forEach((tooltip, index) => {
        const escaped = tooltip.searchString.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&');
        const regex = new RegExp(`(?<=[\\b\\s]|^)${escaped}(?=[.,;!?]?(?:[\\s\\b]|$))`, 'g');
        let match;
        while ((match = regex.exec(str)) !== null) {
            matches.push({
                start: match.index,
                end: match.index + match[0].length,
                tooltipIndex: index
            });
        }
    });
    matches.sort((a, b) => a.start - b.start || b.end - b.start - (a.end - a.start));
    for (let i = 0; i < matches.length - 1; ) {
        if (matches[i + 1].start < matches[i].end) {
            matches.splice(i + 1, 1);
        } else {
            i++;
        }
    }
    return matches;
}

function applyTooltips(str) {
    const matches = getTooltips(str);
    let result = '';
    let lastIndex = 0;
    matches.forEach(match => {
        const tooltip = tooltipList[match.tooltipIndex];
        result += str.slice(lastIndex, match.start);
        result += `<span class='mytooltip' style='position:relative'>${tooltip.searchString}${generatePenStroke()}<span class='mytooltiptext'>${tooltip.img ? `<img src='${tooltip.img}'/>` : ''}<span class='tt-label'>${tooltip.label}</span><span class='tt-body'><span class='tt-body-text'>${tooltip.body}</span></span></span></span>`;
        lastIndex = match.end;
    });
    result += str.slice(lastIndex);
    return result;
}

function applyTooltipsToObject(obj) {
    for (let key in obj) {
        if (typeof obj[key] === 'string') {
            obj[key] = applyTooltips(obj[key]);
        } else if (typeof obj[key] === 'object' && obj[key] !== null) {
            applyTooltipsToObject(obj[key]);
        }
    }
}

applyTooltipsToObject(campaignTrail_temp.questions_json);
applyTooltipsToObject(campaignTrail_temp.answers_json);
applyTooltipsToObject(campaignTrail_temp.answer_feedback_json);

const _tooltipPortal = document.createElement('div');
_tooltipPortal.id = 'tooltip-portal';
document.body.appendChild(_tooltipPortal);

let _hoveredTooltip = null;

document.addEventListener('mouseover', (e) => {
    const src = e.target.closest('.mytooltip');
    if (src === _hoveredTooltip) return;
    _hoveredTooltip = src;
    if (src) {
        const inner = src.querySelector('.mytooltiptext');
        if (inner) _tooltipPortal.innerHTML = inner.innerHTML;
    } else {
        _tooltipPortal.style.display = 'none';
    }
});

document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
    if (!_hoveredTooltip) return;
    _tooltipPortal.style.display = 'block';
    const pad = 16;
    const tw = _tooltipPortal.offsetWidth;
    const th = _tooltipPortal.offsetHeight;
    let x = e.clientX + pad;
    let y = e.clientY + pad;
    if (x + tw > window.innerWidth) x = e.clientX - tw - pad;
    if (y + th > window.innerHeight) y = e.clientY - th - pad;
    _tooltipPortal.style.left = x + 'px';
    _tooltipPortal.style.top = y + 'px';
});

document.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
    _tooltipPortal.style.display = 'none';
    _hoveredTooltip = null;
}, true);

const _shownTransitions = new Set();

function showSectionTransition(t, pk) {
    if (_shownTransitions.has(pk)) return;
    _shownTransitions.add(pk);

    const overlay = document.createElement('div');
    overlay.id = 'section-transition-' + pk;
    overlay.style.cssText = `
        position: absolute;
        top: 0; left: 0; width: 989px; height: 625px;
        background-image: url('https://file.garden/aXPgNT-ZRCxxpy0g/background.png');
        background-size: cover; background-position: center;
        z-index: 500;
        display: flex; flex-direction: column;
        align-items: center; justify-content: center;
        text-align: center; padding: 40px; box-sizing: border-box;
        animation: blurtosharp 1s ease-in forwards;
        pointer-events: all;
    `;

    const dismissId = 'section-transition-' + pk;
    const titleLen = t.title.length;
    const typeDuration = (titleLen * 0.25).toFixed(2);
    overlay.innerHTML = `
        <style>
            #${dismissId} h2 {
                overflow: hidden;
                border-right: .15em solid orange;
                white-space: nowrap;
                animation: typing ${typeDuration}s steps(${titleLen}, end),
                           blink-caret .5s step-end infinite;
            }
        </style>
        <h2 style="font-family:'TypewriterDry',sans-serif;font-size:24px;letter-spacing:0.2em;
                   text-transform:uppercase;margin-top:-20px;margin-bottom:34px;">${t.title}</h2>
        <p style="font-family:'TypewriterDry',sans-serif;font-size:14px;max-width:600px;
                  line-height:1.5;margin-bottom:${t.img ? '24px' : '36px'};">${t.body}</p>
        ${t.img ? `<img src="${t.img}" style="display:block;max-width:400px;height:auto;margin:0 auto 36px auto;">` : ''}
        <button onclick="document.getElementById('${dismissId}').remove();">Continue</button>
    `;

    const target = document.getElementById('game_window');
    if (target) {
        target.style.position = 'relative';
        target.appendChild(overlay);
    }
}

function fadeText(el, newText) {
    el.style.transition = 'opacity 0.25s ease';
    el.style.opacity = '0';
    setTimeout(() => {
        el.textContent = newText;
        el.style.opacity = '1';
    }, 150);
}

function attachDateToProgressBar(date, qNum, pk) {
    if (!date) return;
    const h3 = document.querySelector('#progress_bar h3');
    if (!h3) return;
    const total = campaignTrail_temp.global_parameter_json[0].fields.question_count;
    const questionInfo = 'Question ' + (qNum + 1) + ' of ' + total;
    h3.dataset.dateAttached = String(pk);
    h3.textContent = questionInfo;
    h3.style.cursor = 'default';
    h3.addEventListener('pointerenter', () => fadeText(h3, date));
    h3.addEventListener('pointerleave', () => fadeText(h3, questionInfo));
}

function injectHistoricalButton(noFeedbackBtn, pk) {
    noFeedbackBtn.dataset.historicalHooked = 'true';
    noFeedbackBtn.style.display = 'none';
    const histBtn = document.createElement('button');
    histBtn.id = 'historical_button';
    histBtn.textContent = 'Historical';
    histBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        const qd = (pk != null && questionData[pk]) || {};
        showHistoricalPanel(qd.historical);
    });
    noFeedbackBtn.insertAdjacentElement('afterend', histBtn);
}

function showHistoricalPanel(data) {
    const existing = document.getElementById('historical-panel');
    if (existing) existing.remove();

    const panel = document.createElement('div');
    panel.id = 'historical-panel';
    panel.innerHTML = `
        <h2>Historical Context</h2>
        <div id="historical-panel-body">
            ${data ? data : '<p class="historical-placeholder">Historical context coming soon.</p>'}
        </div>
        <button id="historical-panel-back">Back</button>
    `;
    panel.querySelector('#historical-panel-back').addEventListener('click', () => panel.remove());

    const target = document.getElementById('game_window');
    if (target) target.appendChild(panel);
}

let nixonClickCount = 0;
let nixonClickTimer = null;

document.body.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
    if (!e.target.closest('#candidate_pic')) return;
    nixonClickCount++;
    if (nixonClickTimer) clearTimeout(nixonClickTimer);
    nixonClickTimer = setTimeout(() => { nixonClickCount = 0; }, 10000);
    if (nixonClickCount >= 3) {
        nixonClickCount = 0;
        clearTimeout(nixonClickTimer);
        const audio = document.getElementById('audio');
        const crook = new Audio (window.konamiActive
        ? 'https://file.garden/aXPgNT-ZRCxxpy0g/drunkasever.mp3'
        : 'https://file.garden/aXPgNT-ZRCxxpy0g/Richard_Nixon_-__I\'m_not_a_crook._.mp3');
        if (audio) audio.muted = true;
        crook.play();
        crook.addEventListener('ended', () => {
            if (audio) audio.muted = false;
        }, { once: true });
    }
});
let agnewClickCount = 0;
let agnewClickTimer = null;

document.body.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
    if (!e.target.closest('#running_mate_pic')) return;
    agnewClickCount++;
    if (agnewClickTimer) clearTimeout(agnewClickTimer);
    agnewClickTimer = setTimeout(() => { agnewClickCount = 0; }, 10000);
    if (agnewClickCount >= 3) {
        agnewClickCount = 0;
        clearTimeout(agnewClickTimer);
        const audio = document.getElementById('audio');
        const nabobs = new Audio(window.konamiActive

        if (audio) audio.muted = true;

let honkClickCount = 0;
let honkClickTimer = null;

document.body.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
    if (!e.target.closest('#honk')) return;
    honkClickCount++;
    if (honkClickTimer) clearTimeout(honkClickTimer);
    honkClickTimer = setTimeout(() => { honkClickCount = 0; }, 10000);
    if (honkClickCount >= 2) {
        honkClickCount = 0;
        clearTimeout(honkClickTimer);
        const audio = document.getElementById('audio');
        const honk = new Audio('https://file.garden/aXPgNT-ZRCxxpy0g/Classic%20Car%20Horn%20Sound%20Effect%20Best%20Audio%20Quality.mp3');
        if (audio) audio.muted = true;
        honk.play();
        honk.addEventListener('ended', () => {
            if (audio) audio.muted = false;
        }, { once: true });
    }
});

const honk = document.createElement('div');
honk.id = 'honk';
honk.style.cssText = `
    position: absolute;
    left: 1598px;
    top: 748px;
    width: 100px;
    height: 155px;
    z-index: 9999;
    cursor: pointer;
    background: transparent;
`;

const konamiCode = ['ArrowUp','ArrowUp','ArrowDown','ArrowDown','ArrowLeft','ArrowRight','ArrowLeft','ArrowRight','b','a'];
let konamiIndex = 0;

document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
    if (e.key === konamiCode[konamiIndex]) {
        konamiIndex++;
        if (konamiIndex === konamiCode.length) {
            konamiIndex = 0;
            const candPic = document.getElementById('candidate_pic');
            const matePic = document.getElementById('running_mate_pic');
            if (candPic) candPic.src = 'https://file.garden/aXPgNT-ZRCxxpy0g/konaminixon.png';
            if (matePic) matePic.src = 'https://file.garden/aXPgNT-ZRCxxpy0g/konamiagnew.png';
            window.konamiActive = true;
            const headerImg = document.getElementById('header');
            if (headerImg) headerImg.src = 'https://file.garden/aXPgNT-ZRCxxpy0g/oldfreebie.png';
        }
    } else {
        konamiIndex = 0;
    }
});
document.body.appendChild(honk);

;(() => {
    /* Load Permanent Marker from Google Fonts */
    if (!document.getElementById('fd-pm-font')) {
        const l = document.createElement('link');
        l.id = 'fd-pm-font';
        l.rel = 'stylesheet';
        l.href = 'https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Permanent+Marker&display=swap';
        document.head.appendChild(l);
    }

    /* ── CSS ── */
    const _fdStyle = document.createElement('style');
    _fdStyle.textContent = `
    #fd-overlay {
        position: fixed;
        inset: 0;
        z-index: 9000;
        background: rgba(40,20,0,.4);
        pointer-events: none; /* backdrop doesn't block; fd-inner handles its own events */
    }
    .fd-inner {
        position: absolute; /* placed by JS; draggable */
        width: 580px;
        max-height: 88vh;
        display: flex;
        flex-direction: column;
        filter: drop-shadow(4px 8px 22px rgba(0,0,0,.7));
    }
    .fd-tabs-row {
        display: flex;
        align-items: flex-end;
        gap: 2px;
        padding-left: 14px;
        pointer-events: all;
    }
    .fd-tab {
        all: unset;
        box-sizing: border-box;
        display: inline-block;
        padding: 5px 15px 7px;
        background: #a07028;
        border-radius: 5px 5px 0 0;
        border: 1.5px solid #6b400a;
        border-bottom: 2px solid #a07028; /* inactive: solid bottom seam */
        cursor: pointer;
        font-family: 'TypewriterDry', 'Courier New', monospace;
        font-size: 11px;
        color: #2a1200;
        letter-spacing: .05em;
        user-select: none;
    }
    .fd-tab:not(.fd-active):hover { background: #b88030; border-bottom-color: #b88030; }
    .fd-tab.fd-active {
        background: #d4a843;
        border-bottom: 2px solid #d4a843; /* active: blends into body */
        color: #110500;
        font-size: 12px;
        position: relative;
        top: 1px;
    }
    .fd-body {
        flex: 1;
        background: #d4a843;
        background-image: linear-gradient(148deg,
            rgba(255,230,120,.25) 0%,
            transparent 40%,
            rgba(0,0,0,.06) 100%);
        border: 2px solid #6b400a;
        border-radius: 0 10px 10px 10px;
        padding: 10px;
        position: relative;
        overflow: hidden;
        cursor: grab;
    }
    .fd-body:active { cursor: grabbing; }
    .fd-close {
        position: absolute;
        top: 7px; right: 10px;
        background: none;
        border: none;
        font-family: 'TypewriterDry', monospace;
        font-size: 18px;
        color: #5a3300;
        cursor: pointer;
        line-height: 1;
        padding: 0 4px;
        z-index: 1;
    }
    .fd-close:hover { color: #110500; }
    .fd-pad {
        background-color: #fdf4b0;
        background-image:
            linear-gradient(90deg,
                transparent 46px,
                #e57373 46px, #e57373 48px,
                transparent 48px),
            repeating-linear-gradient(180deg,
                transparent 0px,
                transparent 27px,
                #90caf9 27px,
                #90caf9 28.5px);
        border: 1px solid #b89820;
        border-radius: 3px;
        padding: 12px 14px 24px 60px;
        max-height: calc(88vh - 90px);
        overflow-y: auto;
        box-shadow: inset 1px 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,.10);
        scrollbar-width: thin;
        cursor: default; /* override grab from fd-body */
    }
    .fd-head {
        font-family: 'TypewriterDry', 'Courier New', monospace !important;
        font-size: 19px !important;
        color: #1a0800 !important;
        margin: 4px 0 20px !important;
        letter-spacing: .04em;
        text-decoration: underline;
        text-underline-offset: 4px;
        line-height: 28px;
    }
    .fd-entry { margin-bottom: 22px; }
    .fd-entry-label {
        font-family: 'TypewriterDry', 'Courier New', monospace;
        font-size: 11px;
        font-weight: bold;
        color: #5a3300;
        display: block;
        text-transform: uppercase;
        letter-spacing: .1em;

        font-family: 'TypewriterDry', 'Courier New', monospace;
        font-size: 11px;
        color: #7b3f00;
        text-transform: uppercase;
        letter-spacing: .06em;

        line-height: 28px;
    }
    .fd-empty {
        font-family: 'TypewriterDry', 'Courier New', monospace !important;

    #btn_game_stats { margin-left: 1.5em; }
    `;
    document.head.appendChild(_fdStyle);

    /* ── State of the Nation stats ── */
    function _bold(text, color) {
        return `<span style="color:${color};font-weight:bold">${text}</span>`;
    }
    function _matchTier(v, tiers) {
        for (const [max, text, color] of tiers) if (v <= max) return [text, color];
        const f = tiers.at(-1);
        return [f?.[1] || '', f?.[2] || '#444'];
    }
    const _STATS = [
        {
            getValue: () => MentalState,
            label: 'Mental State',
            tiers: [
                [2,        "Prefers to have the blinds closed", "#c0392b"],
                [7,        "Talking to paintings",              "#555555"],
                [Infinity, "No longer the madman 'theory'",    "#1a7340"],
            ],
        },
        {
            getValue: () => ApprovalRating,
            label: 'Approval Rating',
            tiers: [
                [40,       "Approval Rating is struggling", "#c0392b"],
                [60,       "Approval Rating is steady",     "#555555"],
                [Infinity, "Historic approval levels",      "#1a7340"],
            ],
        },
    ];

    /* ── High Crimes log ── */
    window._hcEvents = [
        { date: 'Jun 17, 1972', text: 'Operatives from CREEP arrested inside the Watergate complex.' },
        { date: 'Jun 23, 1972', text: "The President instructs Haldeman to use the CIA to obstruct the FBI's Watergate investigation. The cover-up begins." },
    ];
    window._hcLog = (text, date) => {
        window._hcEvents.push({ date: date || '', text });
        _refresh();
    };

    /* ── Render ── */
    function _buildNation() {
        let h = `<p class="fd-head">State of the Nation</p>`;
        for (const { getValue, label, tiers } of _STATS) {
            const v = Number(getValue?.()) || 0;
            const [text, color] = _matchTier(v, tiers);
            h += `<div class="fd-entry"><span class="fd-entry-label">${label}</span>`;
            h += `<span class="fd-entry-body">${_bold(text, color)} (${v})</span></div>`;
        }
        return h;
    }

    function _buildCrimes() {
        let h = `<p class="fd-head">High Crimes &amp; Misdemeanours</p>`;
        if (!window._hcEvents.length) {
            h += `<p class="fd-empty">No entries yet.</p>`;
        } else {
            for (const ev of window._hcEvents) {
                h += `<div class="fd-crime-entry">`;
                if (ev.date) h += `<span class="fd-crime-date">${ev.date}</span>`;
                h += `<span class="fd-entry-body">${ev.text}</span></div>`;
            }
        }
        return h;
    }

    function _refresh() {
        const pad = document.getElementById('fd-pad');
        if (!pad) return;
        const which = document.querySelector('.fd-tab.fd-active')?.dataset.tab;
        if (which === 'nation') pad.innerHTML = _buildNation();
        else if (which === 'crimes') pad.innerHTML = _buildCrimes();
    }

    /* ── Drag ── */
    function _makeDraggable(el) {
        let ox, oy;
        el.addEventListener('mousedown', ev => {
            if (ev.target.closest('.fd-pad, .fd-close, .fd-tab')) return;
            const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
            ox = ev.clientX - rect.left;
            oy = ev.clientY - rect.top;
            function onMove(ev) {
                const maxX = window.innerWidth  - el.offsetWidth;
                const maxY = window.innerHeight - el.offsetHeight;
                el.style.left = `${Math.max(0, Math.min(ev.clientX - ox, maxX))}px`;
                el.style.top  = `${Math.max(0, Math.min(ev.clientY - oy, maxY))}px`;
            }
            function onUp() {
                document.removeEventListener('mousemove', onMove);
                document.removeEventListener('mouseup',  onUp);
            }
            document.addEventListener('mousemove', onMove);
            document.addEventListener('mouseup',  onUp);
            ev.preventDefault();
        });
    }

    /* ── Open / close ── */
    function _open() {
        if (document.getElementById('fd-overlay')) return;

        const ov = document.createElement('div');
        ov.id = 'fd-overlay';

        const inner = document.createElement('div');
        inner.className = 'fd-inner';
        inner.style.pointerEvents = 'all';
        /* centre on open */
        inner.style.left = `${Math.max(0, Math.floor((window.innerWidth - 580) / 2))}px`;
        inner.style.top  = `${Math.max(0, Math.floor(window.innerHeight * 0.08))}px`;
        _makeDraggable(inner);

        const tabRow = document.createElement('div');
        tabRow.className = 'fd-tabs-row';

        [
            { label: 'State of the Nation',         key: 'nation' },
            { label: 'High Crimes & Misdemeanours', key: 'crimes' },
        ].forEach(({ label, key }, i) => {
            const t = document.createElement('button');
            t.className = 'fd-tab' + (i === 0 ? ' fd-active' : '');
            t.dataset.tab = key;
            t.textContent = label;
            t.onclick = () => {
                document.querySelectorAll('.fd-tab').forEach(x => x.classList.remove('fd-active'));
                t.classList.add('fd-active');
                _refresh();
            };
            tabRow.appendChild(t);
        });

        const body = document.createElement('div');
        body.className = 'fd-body';

        const closeBtn = document.createElement('button');
        closeBtn.className = 'fd-close';
        closeBtn.innerHTML = '&#x2715;';
        closeBtn.onclick = _close;
        body.appendChild(closeBtn);

        const pad = document.createElement('div');
        pad.className = 'fd-pad';
        pad.id = 'fd-pad';
        pad.innerHTML = _buildNation();
        body.appendChild(pad);

        inner.appendChild(tabRow);
        inner.appendChild(body);
        ov.appendChild(inner);
        document.body.appendChild(ov);
    }

    function _close() {
        document.getElementById('fd-overlay')?.remove();
    }

    /* ── Button ── */
    function _injectBtn() {
        if (document.getElementById('btn_game_stats')) return;
        const anchor = document.getElementById('view_electoral_map');
        if (!anchor) return;
        const btn = document.createElement('button');
        btn.id = 'btn_game_stats';
        btn.textContent = 'Legal Pad';
        btn.addEventListener('click', _open);
        anchor.insertAdjacentElement('afterend', btn);
    }

    const gw = document.getElementById('game_window');
    if (gw) {
        new MutationObserver(() => {
            _injectBtn();
            _refresh();
        }).observe(gw, { childList: true, subtree: true });
    }
})();
// [JETS_CYOA_CAMPAIGN_DATA_END]
//#endcode
